         </li>

      <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-md-push-3" id="main_content">
       <div class="main-inner">
        <div class="widget">
         <h1 class="widget-title">
          Mai Chau , Nghia Lo, Mu Cang Chai , Sapa 8 days
         </h1>
         <div class="page-content">
          <div class="page-content-inner">
           <div class="clearfix arw_prod_details">
            <div class="arw_prod_details_left">
             <a class="arw-fancybox" href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/sapa1.jpg" title="Mai Chau , Nghia Lo, Mu Cang Chai , Sapa 8 days">
              <img alt="sapa1" class="img-thumbnail img-responsive wp-post-image" height="200" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/sapa1-300x200.jpg" width="300"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="arw_prod_details_right">
             <p class="clearfix">
              <span>
               Tour code
              </span>
              <span>
               TH00118
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="clearfix">
              <span>
               Price
              </span>
              <span>
               Contact Us
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="clearfix">
              <span>
               Duration
              </span>
              <span>
               8 Days
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="clearfix">
              <span>
               Tour route
              </span>
              <span>
               Hanoi - Mai Chau - Nghia Lo - Mu Cang Chai - Sapa
              </span>
             </p>
             <div class="clearfix prod_action">
              <button class="btn" data-id="2553" data-post-type="tour">
               <span>
                Book now
               </span>
              </button>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="clearfix">
            <h2>
             Details
            </h2>
            <div class="clearfix">
            </div>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Mountains covered with thick rain forest, lush plantation, wild nature and friendly people from different ethnic minority groups with their colorful and fantastic culture and custom That is all this untouched area offers. However, this trip is for those who are brave and ready to sacrifice time, energy and city modern facilities to the exploring wild nature as well as discovering diversified culture of the ethnic minority peoples.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Basically use vehicle for the whole trip but walking and trekking is quite regularly and flexible for your decision. Accommodation for the whole trip is in standard hotels guesthouses and village home stay.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mai-Chau-pu-Luong11.jpg">
               <img align="right" alt="mai Chau pu Luong1" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-2554" height="210" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mai-Chau-pu-Luong11.jpg" style="margin-left: 10px;" width="350"/>
              </a>
             </span>
             <br/>
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 1: Hanoi  Mai Chau
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Departing from Hanoi, we cross the western edge of the Red River Delta with lively scenery of the countryside. After 70 km, the road gradually ascends uphill through the region of the Muong ethnic and suddenly it goes up steep mountains and view of the lush valley opens wider and wider. We stop for admiring the marvelous panorama scenery before descending to the valley and arrive in a large village of the Thai ethnic group. It is well organized and prosperous village as many others in the region with wooden houses on stilts standing in lines. All the houses are spacious with palm leaf roof and bamboo slat floor, the kitchen is set at one end of the house.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Although living in the mountainous region, The Thai people always choose the low land with permanent sources of water for rice intensive farming. Thai women are famous for their weaving and embroidering skill to make brocade.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              We spent the rest of the day walking and exploring villages, meeting local doing their everyday works and experiencing wonderful hospitality of the Thai people.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Most interesting of all is the overnight stay in a villagers house, attending the traditional dance performed by the Thai people, a truly remarkable and unforgettable event.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mai-Chau-pu-Luong31.jpg">
              <img align="right" alt="mai Chau pu Luong3" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-2555" height="203" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mai-Chau-pu-Luong31.jpg" style="margin-left: 10px;" width="353"/>
             </a>
             <br/>
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 2: Mai Chau  Suoi Lon
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Today you will explore an untouched area. After Breakfast, you will leave Ban Lac of the Thai for a short drive for about half an hour. The trek takes about 4 hours up and down hill and then pass through a prosperous valley inhabited by Thai and Hmong ethnic. In Hang Kia and Cun Pheo villages you have chances to visit Hmong families those just started to settle for few years after practicing slash and burn agriculture for generations. Later the path gradually getting to the lower land as you approach to the Da River. Here, boarding a boat and cruise upstream the river for over 3 hours to explore wild life and meet Muong people who earn a living by fishing around this area of the Reservoir. Arriving at Suoi Lon Village of the Muong in the afternoon, you will join the locals work for your experience of local life. Home stay in the village.
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 3: Suoi Lon  Bac Yen  Thu Cuc
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Enjoy a morning short walk out of the Mount village and our jeep and driver will pick us up for a two hours transfer through beautiful area with rich farmland covered by tea plantations, fancy some side visit to ethnic villages along the way and seeing tea processing. We have long break at noon in a little pretty town Ta Sua, a local center where we have Lunch and walk around the market which is colorful with local farming produces as will as minority handicrafts. Later we take a walk for about 5 km along a track passing villages of Thai and Muong, tea farms, fantastic scenery. Visiting some local homes and tasting local wine which is fermented in pottery jar.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Arriving in Thu Cuc where we stay overnight in another Muong Village.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Nghia-lo.jpg">
              <img align="right" alt="Nghia lo" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-2556" height="208" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Nghia-lo.jpg" style="margin-left: 10px;" width="358"/>
             </a>
             <br/>
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 4: Thu Cuc  Nghia Lo
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              The terrain changes today as we drive to Nghia Lo, Starting from Thu Cuc, featuring with fertile hilly area covered with green tea plantations, the mountains get higher and higher. Along the way you can see thick forests cover high mountains. Spending about 4 hours walking through a narrow and long valley, we meet three tribal setting their villages in different ways which reveal their traditional customs and living style: The Thai occupy the low land almost at bottom of valleys, near river or streams from which they build up water wheels for transfer water to rice paddies on which they farm wet rice intensively. The Hmong settle at the highest elevation, grow corn and dry rice on the burn-over land and the Zao live in the middle practice both methods of farming and it is easily to realize that they learn a lot of farming technique from the Thai.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Arriving in Nghia Lo, a pretty mountainous town, we spend the remaining hours of the day wandering the town including the market area.
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 5: Nghia Lo  Tu Le
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              It is not far from Nghia Lo to Tu Le. The road ride today takes only 2 hours so we have a lot of time exploring the area for real mountainous life of the local ethnic minority people. Fancy a four hour trekking along a trail which connect villages to villages, meeting different tribal people such as White Thai, Black Zao, Red Hmongwho seem very surprise, staring at you for the first moment and turn out very friendly and inviting you to their homes in which you will be hosted with tea or home made wine.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              We enjoy another home staying in a large Thai village, which offers fantastic hours for your culture discovery.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mu-cang-chai.jpg">
              <img align="right" alt="mu cang chai" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-2557" height="210" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/mu-cang-chai.jpg" style="margin-left: 10px;" width="350"/>
             </a>
             <br/>
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 6: Tu Le  Mu Cang Chai  Than Uyen
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              We are heading uphill to Hoang Lien Son range of mountains, the roof of Indochina, for our discovery from the back side of this famous area. The Northeast of this range, consider the front side with Sa Pa has been known and become popular tourist destination for almost 2 decades but the back side is staying unknown to many, even local travelers talking of the area which we are going today as of another world.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              The first tip of the day is the morning market at the center of Tu Le. Tribal peoples from remotest villages in their traditional costumes which are very different from one another go to market with cheerful faceswhich makes you surprise!
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Leaving the market for a short drive, you will find yourselves in the magnificent area of this unspoiled area, Kau Pha. From the foot of this mountain pass, we challenge a 9 km trek through thick jungle up to the top of the pass which is at 1,800m above sea level. Enjoy fresh air and great view.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              After Lunch in Mu Cang Chai town, we continue our drive uphill which offers even more spectacular scenery, far away from what you expect!
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Arriving in Than Uyen town late in the afternoon, check in and relax in the only local guesthouse.
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 7: Than Uyen  Binh Lu  Sapa
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              We slowly drive along the foot of Fansipan, admiring its magnificence and beauty from the west side which is often clearer in comparison with that from Sa Pa at the east side. Today you will meet people from Lu minority whose population is just about 5000. Some old Lu men said that their ancestors came to settle in the region from Laos many years ago and they adopted rice farming style of the Thai while maintaining their traditional culture which reveals on womens clothes and jewelry and still keep dying their teeth black.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              The 60 km drive from Binh Lu to Sa Pa offers the most spectacular scenery in Vietnam for sure.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              It is hard work to driver because beautiful landscapes makes you wish to stop at every corner while going up steep road!
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Arriving in Sa Pa in the afternoon, you will spend the rest of the day wandering around the narrow and busy old street of this
              <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/location/sapa-tours/" target="_blank" title="famous destinations">
               famous tourist destination
              </a>
              .
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Day 8: Sapa villages explore  Overnight train back to Hanoi
              </span>
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Sapa-Ha-Giang3.jpg">
              <img align="right" alt="Sapa Ha Giang3" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-2562" height="210" src="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/Sapa-Ha-Giang3.jpg" style="margin-left: 10px;" width="350"/>
             </a>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Most other tourists come from Hanoi will be anxious for trips to explore tribal villages around Sapa town but not you! Because these trips can not compare with what you had experienced so far. So the plan today is set open for your flexibility.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              However we suggest a morning trip to visit Lao Chai and Ta Van to admire scenery of Muong Hoa Valley, the most beautiful one from the east side of Fansipan. Car and guide will pick you up at hotel and drive 12 km to the center of the valley where you will enjoy an easy walk along the river, paying visit to Black Hmong and Zay villages for about 3 hours. Drive back to hotel and free to relax.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
              Late afternoon, you will pick up for a road transfer downhill to Lao Cai station for taking the overnight train to Hanoi, which arrives early next morning. Pick up and transfer to your
              <a href="http://vietnamtypicaltours.com/categoryhotel/vietnam-hotels/" target="_blank" title="Hotel in Hanoi">
               hotel in Hanoi
              </a>
              .
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Tour price includes
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               Transfer with private 4 WD car as indicated in day by day itinerary.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               One way overnight train from Lao Cai to Hanoi in first class 4 bed cabin with air-conditioning
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               One way flight tickets from Hanoi to Dien Bien Phu
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               Accommodation: 4 nights home stay at villages, 3 nights in hotel and guesthouse as stated.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               All meals as listed in day by day itinerary.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               Visiting fee, tax and service charge.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               English speaking tour guide.
             </span>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: justify;">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #ff0000;">
               Tour price excludes
              </span>
             </strong>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               Meals not indicated in day by day itinerary.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #000080;">
               Drinks and personal expenses.
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>

       <div class="sidebar-inner">
        <div class="widget widget_nav_menu" id="nav_menu-5">
         <h2 class="widget-title">
